               S13:00001FA5:  3A

F04:0059           dc.b    $0F,$42,$3F                     ; 1st Nybble: Starting location (0=Shion's House, 1=Alsedo, 2=Castle, 3=Lily
F04:0060                                                   ; 2nd Nybble + 2 Bytes = 999999 Gold
F04:0061           endif
F04:0062           ;
F04:0063           ifne CHEAT_HEARTS
F04:0064           org     $8E4A                           ; Cheat: Have all Hearts upon New Game start
F04:0065           dc.b    $8
F04:0066           endif
F04:0067           ;
F04:0068           ifne CHEAT_INVINC

               S14:0000E0A4:  4E 71
F04:0071           nop 
               S14:0000E0A6:  4E 71
F04:0072           endif

F04:0078           ;nop                                     ; with nops
F04:0079           ;endr
F04:0080                                                   ; (i) $70F0.w: Skip SubRoutine to Load Plane A Map to C000-CFFF
F04:0081                                                   ; (i) $70FE.w: Skip SubRoutine to Load Plane B Map to E000-EFFF

F06:0017

               S61:000A4C96:  D2 88
F06:0019           cmp.l   #locSpriteTable_logo,d1         ; Compare address in D1 to original sprite table location
               S61:000A4C98:  B2 BC 00 0A 0E 00
F06:0020           beq     setNewSpriteTable_logo          ; If it matches, branch to set a custom address
               S61:000A4C9E:  67 22
F06:0021           cmp.l   #locSpriteTable_arrow,d1        ; Compare address in D1 to original sprite table location
               S61:000A4CA0:  B2 BC 00 0A 18 E7

               S61:000A4CA6:  67 22

               S61:000A4CA8:  B2 BC 00 0A 18 C8

               S61:000A4CAE:  67 22

               S61:000A4CB0:  B2 BC 00 0A 18 A8
F06:0026           beq     setNewSpriteTable_newGame       ; If it matches, branch to set a custom address
               S61:000A4CB6:  67 22
F06:0027           cmp.l   #locSpriteTable_continue,d1     ; Compare address in D1 to original sprite table location
               S61:000A4CB8:  B2 BC 00 0A 18 B8
F06:0028           beq     setNewSpriteTable_continue      ; If it matches, branch to set a custom address
               S61:000A4CBE:  67 22

               S61:000A4CC0:  60 26

F10:0004       
F10:0005       cc_close            equ $00     ; Closes the textbox
F10:0006       cc_text             equ $01     ; Text Color setter,
F10:0007                                       ; format: 01.b 0RGB.w
F10:0008       cc_textOrange       equ $01A0
F10:0009       cc_textWhite        equ $0180
F10:0010       cc_fast             equ $02     ; Changes the write speed to 'fast'
F10:0011       cc_speed            equ $03     ; Changes the write speed to given value,
F10:0012                                       ; format 03 value.b: 00=fastest, 09=slowest
F10:0013       
F10:0014       cc_margin           equ $04     ; sets textbox margin
F10:0015                                       ; format 04 value.b, where value equals value*tilewidth=8 pixels
F10:0016       
F10:0017       cc_wait             equ $05     ; Displays arrow and waits for user input
F10:0018       cc_jump             equ $06     ; Jumps to a text location
F10:0019                                       ; format: 06.b pointer.w
F10:0020       cc_lock             equ $07     ; disables fast forward of text
F10:0021       cc_newline          equ $09     ; Starts a new line in the textbox
F10:0022       
F10:0023       orange              equ $A0 
F10:0024       white               equ $80
